Anyway, I am extremely tired and I want to sleep for 12 hours! 
But I know that there will be another thunderstorm in Guangdong on the 4th, and the plane will be delayed again. Forget it, go according to the plan and leave at 6 o'clock tomorrow morning. This character of going according to the plan has hurt me. 
Dear friends, do you know what this hotel is like? It is no different from the Shangri-La hotel I stayed in. It is a Chinese-style five-star hotel with five-star standards in facilities, hygiene, and environment. The front desk service when arriving and leaving the hotel, and the after-sales telephone follow-up are all standardized like the five-star hotels I have stayed in! 
I chose this hotel because I thought it was more than ten kilometers away from the airport, but in fact it is also very convenient to go to the city. The main reason is that Binhai Airport is not on the seaside, it is on the edge of Dongli District. After passing Dongli District, you will reach the six central districts: Hedong, Hexi, Hebei, Heping, Nankai, and Hongqiao.
Sometimes it is really not good to not make a travel guide. I always choose to live in Hedong District, thinking that it is better to be close to Haihe River, but I missed the treasure hotel.

advantage:

2. The hotel room is very large and clean. The bedding was not stained. The water in the bathing pool is not yellow and cloudy. There are 2 beds, 2 small sofas (single) and TV in the room; the bathroom has a bathtub, shower room, toilet, and washstand.

shortcoming:
